# <a name="removed-or-deprecated-features-in-previous-releases"></a><span data-ttu-id="55380-103">Varasemate versioonide eemaldatud või iganenud funktsioonid</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-103">Removed or deprecated features in previous releases</span></span>

[!include [banner](../includes/banner.md)]

[!include [rename-banner](~/includes/cc-data-platform-banner.md)]

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="55380-104">Seda teemat enam ei uuendata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-104">This topic is no longer updated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="55380-105">Et näha praegust funktsioonide loendit, mis on Finance and Operations rakendustest eemaldatud või aegunud, otsige rakenduse **"Eemaldatud või aegunud funktsioonid"** sisu, mis on seotud teie kasutatava rakendusega.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-105">To see a current list of features that have been removed or deprecated from Finance and Operations apps, search for **"Removed or deprecated features"** content that relates to the app you're using.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="55380-106">Selle teema all kirjeldatakse funktsioone, mis on eemaldatud või mis olid planeeritud eemaldamiseks tootest Dynamics 365 for Finance and Operations ja selle varasematest väljalasetest.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-106">This topic describes features that have been removed or deprecated from Dynamics 365 for Finance and Operations and previous releases of that product.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="55380-107">*Eemaldatud* funktsioon pole tootes enam saadaval.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-107">A *removed* feature is no longer available in the product.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="55380-108">*Aegunud* funktsioon ei ole aktiivses arenduses ja vee võidakse tulevases värskenduses eemaldada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-108">A *deprecated* feature is not in active development and may be removed in a future update.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="55380-109">See loend peaks aitama teil neid eemaldusi ja aegumisi oma plaanides arvesse võtta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-109">This list is intended to help you consider these removals and deprecations for your own planning.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="55380-110">Üksikasjalikku teavet rakenduse Finance and Operationsi rakenduste objektide kohta leiate teemast [Tehnilise teabe aruanded](/dynamics/s-e/global/axtechrefrep_61).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-110">Detailed information about objects in Finance and Operations apps can be found in the [Technical reference reports](/dynamics/s-e/global/axtechrefrep_61).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="55380-111">Saate võrrelda nende aruannete eri versioone, et õppida objektide kohta, mida on igas Finance and Operationsi rakenduste versioonis muudetud või eemaldatud.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-111">You can compare the different versions of these reports to learn about objects that have changed or been removed in each version of Finance and Operations apps.</span></span>

<p><span data-ttu-id="55380-199"><strong>Märkus:</strong> see funktsioon oli varem aegunud ja asendatud Microsoft Azure DevOpsi integratsioonidega.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-199"><strong>Note:</strong> This feature had previously been deprecated and replaced by Microsoft Azure DevOps integrations.</span></span></p>
</li>
<li><span data-ttu-id="55380-200">Vooskeemi versiooniajalugu ei ole saadaval.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-200">The version history of the flowchart will be unavailable.</span></span></li>
</ul>
</td>

### <a name="parameter-to-enable-sales-orders-with-multiple-project-contract-funding-sources"></a><span data-ttu-id="55380-280">Parameeter müügitellimuste lubamiseks mitme projektilepingu rahastamisallikaga</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-280">Parameter to enable sales orders with multiple project contract funding sources</span></span>

| &nbsp;  |&nbsp;  |
|------------|--------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="55380-283">**Aegumise/eemaldamise põhjus**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-283">**Reason for deprecation/removal**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="55380-284">Pärast parameetri eemaldamist on see funktsioon alati lubatud.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-284">The functionality will always be enabled after the parameter is removed.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="55380-285">**Asendatud teise funktsiooniga?**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-285">**Replaced by another feature?**</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="55380-286">Nr</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-286">No.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="55380-287">Mitme rahastamisallikaga projektipõhiste müügitellimuste toetamise funktsioon on alati lubatud.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-287">The functionality to support project-based sales orders with multiple funding sources will always be enabled.</span></span>   |

### <a name="data-partitions"></a><span data-ttu-id="55380-1178">Andmesektsioonid</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-1178">Data partitions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="55380-1179">Andmesektsioonid tagavad andmete loogilise eraldamise Dynamicsi AX andmebaasis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-1179">Data partitions provide a logical separation of data in the Dynamics AX database.</span></span>

| &nbsp;  | &nbsp; |
|------------|--------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="55380-1180">**Aegumise/eemaldamise põhjus**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-1180">**Reason for deprecation/removal**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="55380-1181">Dynamics AX 2012 R2-s võeti andmete eraldamise võimaldamiseks kasutusele andmesektsioonid.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-1181">Data partitions were introduced in Dynamics AX 2012 R2 to enable data isolation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="55380-1182">Tavastsenaariumi puhul on ettevõttel tütarettevõtted ja ühe tütarettevõtte andmed ei tohiks olla teisele tütarettevõttele näha, kuigi mõlemaid tütarettevõtteid haldab sama IT-osakond.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-1182">In a common scenario, a company has subsidiaries, and the data from one subsidiary should not be visible to another subsidiary, even though both subsidiaries are managed by the same IT department.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="55380-1183">Kuid uute sektsioonide loomiseks ja nende täitmiseks andmetega ning sektsiooni andmete varundamiseks oli vaja kogu programmis lisaskripte ja halduse üldkulusid.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-1183">However, extra scripts and management overhead throughout the program were required in order to create new partitions and populate them with data, and to back up partition data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="55380-1184">Pilves, kus meil on juurdepääs platvormi teenusena (PaaS) andmebaasiteenustele (Microsoft Azure SQL-i andmebaas) on palju tõhusam kasutada andmebaasi eralduskonteinerina, kui teha eraldamine programmis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-1184">In the cloud, where we have access to platform as a service (PaaS) database services (Microsoft Azure SQL Database), it's much more efficient to use a database as the isolation container than to do isolation in the program.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="55380-1185">Olenemata sellest, kas andmete eraldamine on vajalik tütarettevõtetele, mitmele rentnikule või lihtsalt skaleerimiseks, usume, et neid stsenaariume saab käsitleda paremini rakenduse Finance and Operations mitme eksemplari kaudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-1185">Regardless of whether data partitioning is required for subsidiaries, for multiple tenants, or just for scale, we believe that the scenarios can be handled better through multiple instances of Finance and Operations.</span></span> |

### <a name="mexican-cfd-electronic-invoice"></a><span data-ttu-id="55380-1372">Mehhiko CFD elektrooniline arve</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-1372">Mexican CFD electronic invoice</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="55380-1373">See funktsioon lubas Mehhiko elektrooniliste arvete loomise, kasutades meetodit Comprobante Fiscal Digital (CFD), kus ettevõte allkirjastab arve, küsides valitsuselt vajalikku kinnitust.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-1373">This feature enabled the generation of Mexican electronic invoices by using the Comprobante Fiscal Digital (CFD) method, where the company signs the invoice by requesting the related authorization from the government.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="55380-1374">See funktsioon pakub ka igakuist aruannet, mis sisaldab kõiki perioodi jooksul väljastatud elektroonilisi arveid.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-1374">This feature also provides a monthly report that includes all electronics invoices that were issued in the period.</span></span>

| &nbsp;  | &nbsp; |
|------------|--------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="55380-1375">**Aegumise/eemaldamise põhjus**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-1375">**Reason for deprecation/removal**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="55380-1376">Seda meetodit ei rakendata enam.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-1376">The method is no longer applicable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="55380-1377">Maksuasutused eemaldasid kasutuselt elektrooniliste arvete koostamise meetodiga CFD ja asendasid selle meetodiga Comprobante Fiscal Digital a través de Internet (CFDI), kus allkirjastamine on delegeeritud muust osapoolest teenusepakkujale (PAC).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-1377">The generation of electronic invoices by using the CFD method was deprecated by the tax authorities and replaced by the Comprobante Fiscal Digital a través de Internet (CFDI) method, where the signing is delegated to the third-party provider (PAC).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="55380-1378">Igakuine aruanne on eemaldatud ja päringu valik võimaldab kasutajatel varasemate kannete kohta päringuid esitada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="55380-1378">The monthly report has been removed, and an inquiry option lets users inquire about historical transactions.</span></span> |
